	# Sept of Baelor Throneroom
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/SeptofBaelor/asoiaf_throneroom_sept_of_baelor.dds"

		trigger = {
			title:b_visenyas_hill.title_province = { has_special_building = yes } #holy_site_great_sept_01
			is_human = yes
			is_in_army = no
			OR = {
				AND = {
					location ?= title:b_visenyas_hill.title_province
					involved_activity ?= {
						OR = {
							has_activity_type = activity_funeral
							has_activity_type = activity_wedding
							has_activity_type = activity_pilgrimage
							has_activity_type = activity_coronation
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						AND = { #High Septon
							exists = location
							has_title = title:k_the_most_devout #is head of the Faith
							#is_theocratic_lessee = yes #HS isn't always a lessee
							location = { geographical_region = world_westeros_the_crownlands } #if in Crownlands, he gets the background
						}
						AND = { #Regular septon leasing the holding
							exists = liege
							liege.capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
							is_theocratic_lessee = yes
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = primary_spouse
					primary_spouse = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_title = title:k_the_most_devout #is head of the Faith
								#is_theocratic_lessee = yes
								location = { geographical_region = world_westeros_the_crownlands } #if in Crownlands, he gets the background
							}
							AND = {
								exists = liege
								liege.capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
								is_theocratic_lessee = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}

				#	exists = betrothed
				#	betrothed = {

				#			AND = {

				#				is_theocratic_lessee = yes
				#			}
				#		}
				#	}

							AND = {
								has_title = title:k_the_most_devout #is head of the Faith
								#is_theocratic_lessee = yes

	# The Citadel throneroom
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/Citadel/asoiaf_throneroom_citadel.dds"

		trigger = {
			title:b_the_citadel.title_province = { has_special_building = yes }
			is_human = yes
			is_in_army = no
			#is_travelling = no #TODO: unless your travel destination IS the Citadel
			OR = {
				AND = {
					location ?= title:b_the_citadel.title_province
					involved_activity ?= {
						OR = {
							has_activity_type = activity_pilgrimage
							has_activity_type = activity_adult_education
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					capital_barony ?= title:b_the_citadel
					has_title = title:b_the_citadel
				}
				AND = {
					exists = primary_spouse
					primary_spouse = {
						NOT = { is_ruler = yes }
						capital_barony ?= title:b_the_citadel
						has_title = title:b_the_citadel
					}
				}
				#AND = {
				#	exists = betrothed
				#	betrothed = {
				#		capital_barony = title:b_the_citadel
				#		has_title = title:b_the_citadel
				#	}
				#}
				AND = {
					exists = host
					host = {
						capital_barony ?= title:b_the_citadel
						has_title = title:b_the_citadel
					}
					NAND = {
						exists = liege
						liege.capital_barony ?= title:b_the_citadel
						is_theocratic_lessee = yes
					}
				}
				# AND = {
				# 	has_title = title:d_kingsguard

	# DUNGEON

	####
	# tribal
	####
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/fp1_tribal_prison.dds"

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_in_prison_type = dungeon }
				imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				is_in_prison_type = house_arrest
				imprisoner = { is_landless_adventurer = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	environment = {
		reference = "environment_event_fp1_tribal_prison"

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_in_prison_type = dungeon }
				imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				is_in_prison_type = house_arrest
				imprisoner = { is_landless_adventurer = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	environment = {
		reference = "environment_event_fp1_tribal_prison"

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				primary_spouse ?= {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { is_in_prison_type = dungeon }
						imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
					}
					trigger_else = {
						is_in_prison_type = house_arrest
						imprisoner = { is_landless_adventurer = yes }
					}
				}
				betrothed ?= {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { is_in_prison_type = dungeon }
						imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
					}
					trigger_else = {
						is_in_prison_type = house_arrest
						imprisoner = { is_landless_adventurer = yes }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					liege.diarch ?= this
					liege ?= {
						trigger_if = {
							limit = { is_in_prison_type = dungeon }
							imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
						}
						trigger_else = {
							is_in_prison_type = house_arrest
							imprisoner = { is_landless_adventurer = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			is_character_window_main_character = no
		}
	}

				}
				AND = {
					liege.diarch ?= this
					liege ?= {
						involved_activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_pilgrimage }
						involved_activity.activity_location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location ?= involved_activity.activity_location
					}
				}
			}
			is_character_window_main_character = no
		}
	}

	# Landless Adventurer Camp
	#####
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/ep3_adventurer_background.dds"

		trigger = {
			government_has_flag = government_is_landless_adventurer
			OR = {
				has_realm_law = camp_purpose_scholars
				liege ?= { has_realm_law = camp_purpose_scholars }
			}
			NOR = {
				is_imprisoned = yes
				#AGOT Modified
				#is_travelling = yes
				agot_is_graphical_travelling_trigger = yes
				exists = involved_activity
			}
		}
	}

	### IRON THRONE THRONEROOM ###
	##############################

	# Iron Throneroom
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/ironthrone/throneroom_ironthrone.dds" #asoiaf_throneroom_redkeep

		trigger = {
			title:b_the_red_keep.title_province = { has_special_building = yes } #holy_site_great_sept_01
			OR = {
				AND = {
					location ?= title:b_the_red_keep.title_province
					involved_activity ?= {
						OR = {
							has_activity_type = activity_feast
							has_activity_type = activity_funeral
							has_activity_type = activity_wedding
							has_activity_type = activity_tour
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = capital_county
					capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
					has_title = title:c_kings_landing
					is_travelling = no
				}
				AND = {
					exists = primary_spouse
					primary_spouse = {
						NOT = { is_ruler = yes }
						exists = capital_county
						capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
						has_title = title:c_kings_landing
					}
				}
				#AND = {
				#	exists = betrothed
				#	betrothed = {
				#		exists = capital_county
				#		capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
				#		has_title = title:c_kings_landing
				#	}
				#}
				AND = {
					exists = host
					host = {
						exists = capital_county
						capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
						has_title = title:c_kings_landing
					}
					NAND = {
						exists = liege
						liege.capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
						is_theocratic_lessee = yes
					}
				}
				# AND = {
				# 	has_title = title:d_kingsguard 
				# 	exists = liege
				# 	liege = {
				# 		has_title = title:c_kings_landing
				# 	}
				# }
			}
		}
	}
	
	environment = {
		reference = "environment_throneroom_iron_throne"

		trigger = {
			title:b_the_red_keep.title_province = { has_special_building = yes } #holy_site_great_sept_01
			OR = {
				AND = {
					location ?= title:b_the_red_keep.title_province
					involved_activity ?= {
						OR = {
							has_activity_type = activity_feast

				AND = {

					exists = primary_spouse

						NOT = { is_ruler = yes }
						exists = capital_county
						capital_county = title:c_kings_landing
						has_title = title:c_kings_landing
					}

						has_graphical_reach_region_trigger = yes

					}
				}

						has_graphical_reach_region_trigger = yes
						NOT = { highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					#AGOT Modified

					#host = {
					agot_get_graphical_host_trigger = yes
					scope:graphical_host ?= {
						exists = capital_province
						has_graphical_reach_region_trigger = yes
						NOT = { highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy }
					}
				}

	# Tribal
	texture = {
		reference = "character_view/throneroom_tribal.dds"

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_in_prison_type = house_arrest }
				imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
			}
			trigger_else = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
		}
	}

	environment = {
		reference = "environment_cw_tribal_main"

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_in_prison_type = house_arrest }
				imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
			}
			trigger_else = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
			is_character_window_main_character = yes
		}
	}

	environment = {
		reference = "environment_cw_tribal_spouse"

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				primary_spouse ?= {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { is_in_prison_type = house_arrest }
						imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
					}
					trigger_else = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
				}
				betrothed ?= {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { is_in_prison_type = house_arrest }
						imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
					}
					trigger_else = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
				}
				AND = {
					liege.diarch ?= this
					liege ?= {
						trigger_if = {
							limit = { is_in_prison_type = house_arrest }
							imprisoner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
						}

		}

			has_graphical_western_region_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	texture = {

		trigger = {

				has_graphical_india_region_trigger = yes
				has_graphical_mena_region_trigger = yes

		reference = "terrain_types/canyon.dds"
	}
	texture = {
		trigger = {
			title_illustration_save_province_temporary = yes
			scope:province = {
				agot_is_highlands_terrain = yes
			}
		}
		reference = "terrain_types/highlands.dds"
	}
	#AGOT End
	# Ultimate fallback
	texture = {
		reference = "terrain_types/plains.dds"
	}
}

### Private location background for a character (mostly interior, but sometimes exterior for flavour)
# This intentionally tries to be different from the 'character_view_bg' because you might see them at the same time
# Used in character memory window
character_private = {
	######################################
	# Dead
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/temple.dds"
		trigger = {
			#AGOT Modified
			#is_alive = no
			OR = {
				is_alive = no
				agot_is_fake_dead = yes
			}
		}
	}

				#AGOT Disabled
				# culture = culture:norse
				# religion = religion:germanic_religion
				has_graphical_scandinavia_region_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	##########################################

	# Tribal, landed
	texture = {
		# Todo [DB]: No real nice picture for a tribal landed character
		reference = "event_scenes/fp1_tribal_temple.dds"

		trigger = {
			exists = primary_title
			government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
		}
	}

	# Tribal
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/fp1_steward_study.dds"

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					exists = host
					host = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = liege
					liege = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}


	##########################################

	# Iberian, landed
	texture = {
		reference = "event_scenes/bp1_relaxing_room_mena.dds"

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_landed = yes
				domicile ?= { is_domicile_type = estate }
			}
			has_graphical_iberia_region_trigger = yes
		}
	}

		}

		}

			is_landed = no
			domicile ?= { is_domicile_type = estate }

		}
	}

	##########################################

	# Eastern, landed
